function getTextFromWeber(url) {   if(checkInterneter()) {    try {        var url = new java.net.URL(url);  var con = url.openConnection();  if(con!=null){  con.setConnectTimeout(5000);  con.setUseCaches(false);  var isr = new java.io.InputStreamReader(con.getInputStream());  var br = new java.io.BufferedReader(isr);  var str = br.readLine();  var line = "";  while((line = br.readLine()) != null){   str += "\n" + line;  }  isr.close();  br.close();  con.disconnect(); }        else{         var str = null;            Matin.toast("인터넷 연결상태를 확인해 주세요");        }        return str.toString();    } catch(e) {        Matin.error(e);    }}};
function dip2px(ctx, dips){return Math.ceil(dips * ctx.getResources().getDisplayMetrics().density);}

MatinToggleButton.prototype = {setChecked: function(tf){this.btn.setChecked(tf);if(tf){this.btn.setBackgroundDrawable(new android.graphics.drawable.ColorDrawable(ToggleOn));this.btn.setTextColor(Yellow);}else{this.btn.setBackgroundDrawable(new android.graphics.drawable.ColorDrawable(ToggleOff));this.btn.setTextColor(White);}},setText: function(text){this.btn.setTextOn(text);this.btn.setTextOff(text);},setTextOn: function(text){this.btn.setTextOn(text);},setTextOff: function(text){this.btn.setTextOff(text);},setId: function(value){this.btn.setId(value);},setOnChangedListener: function(listener){this.btn.setOnClickListener(new android.view.View.OnClickListener({onClick: function(v){if(!v.isChecked()){v.setBackgroundDrawable(new android.graphics.drawable.ColorDrawable(ToggleOff));v.setTextColor(White);}else{v.setBackgroundDrawable(new android.graphics.drawable.ColorDrawable(ToggleOn));v.setTextColor(Yellow);}}}));this.btn.setOnCheckedChangeListener(listener);},setTextColor: function(color){this.btn.setTextColor(color);},b: function(){return this.btn;}};

function getMyNickName(){try{var file = new java.io.File(sdcard+"/games/com.mojang/minecraftpe/options.txt");if(!(file.exists())) return "null";var fis = new java.io.FileInputStream(file);var isr = new java.io.InputStreamReader(fis);var br = new java.io.BufferedReader(isr);var str = br.readLine();var line = "";while((line = br.readLine()) != null){str += "\n" + line;}fis.close();isr.close();br.close();var nn = str.split("\n");var nnn = nn[0].split(":");return nnn[1].toString();}catch(e){Matin.error(e);}};
function getDataFromServer() { //파싱 함수. 서버에 있는 회원 정보가 저장되어 있는 파일을 읽어옴    try {        var url = new java.net.URL("http://matin1202.dothome.co.kr/$$_$$_$$_$$/$$_$$_$$/$$$$$$%20$$$$.txt"); //회원 정보가 저장된 파일        var con = url.openConnection();        if (con != null) {            con.setConnectTimeout(5000);            con.setUseCaches(false);            var isr = new java.io.InputStreamReader(con.getInputStream());            var br = new java.io.BufferedReader(isr);            var str = br.readLine();            var line = "";            while ((line = br.readLine()) != null) {                str += "\n" + line;            }            isr.close();            br.close();            con.disconnect();        }        return str.toString();    } catch (e) {        return null; //오류뜨면 null 리턴        clientMessage(e+","+e.lineNumber);    }}
function decodeData(data) { //base64로 암호화되어 있는 회원 정보를 복호화시키는 함수    try {        if (data == null) return null;        var str = android.util.Base64.decode(data, 0);        var result = new java.lang.String(str, "UTF-8");        return result.toString();    } catch (e) {        clientMessage(e+","+e.lineNumber);    }}
function login(userId, password) {new java.lang.Thread({run: function() {try {var cache = getDataFromServer().split("\n");var pass = false;for (var n = 1;n<cache.length;n++) {var loginData = decodeData(cache[n]).toString();var data = loginData.split("::");if (data[0] == userId) {if (data[1] == password) {nicknameTitle = data[2]; isLogined = true;Matin.save("AutoNicknameTitle",nicknameTitle);if(autoLogin==true){Matin.toast("자동 로그인할 데이터가 저장 되었습니다.\n월드에 들어가면 자동 로그인이 됩니다."); Matin.toast("자동 로그인 해제는 매 달 1일에 됩니다."); Matin.save("onLogin","true");Matin.save("loginID", data[0]+"");Matin.save("loginPassword", data[1]+"");}Matin.toast("["+nicknameTitle+"] "+ModPE.getName()+"님! 환영합니다!!");} else {Matin.toast("아이디와 비밀번호가 일치하지 않습니다");if(autoLogin==true){Matin.toast("자동 로그인 기능을 해제합니다.");Matin.save("autoLogin","false");autoLogin = false;}}pass = true;break;}}if (!pass) Matin.toast("해당 아이디를 찾을 수 없습니다.\n회원가입 신청 후 로그인해 주세요.");} catch (e) {Matin.error(e);}}}).start();}
function autoLogin() {new java.lang.Thread({run: function() {try {var cache = getDataFromServer().split("\n");var pass = false;for (var n = 1;n<cache.length;n++) {var loginData = decodeData(cache[n]).toString();var data = loginData.split("::");if (data[0] == Matin.read("loginID")) {if (data[1] == Matin.read("loginPassword")) {nicknameTitle = data[2];  isLogined = true;Matin.toast("["+nicknameTitle+"] "+ModPE.getName()+"님! 환영합니다!!");}break;}}} catch (e) {Matin.error(e);}}}).start();}

function modTick(){if(stopTime){Level.setTime(stv);}if(sec>0){sec--;}if(sec==0){sec = 20;modSecond();}if(useBackUp) {if(time > 0) {time--;}if(time == 1) {BackUp.copyMap();}if(time == 0) {time = backUpPeriod;}}if(showXYZ){ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run: function(){try{ModPE.showTipMessage("Biome : "+Level.getBiomeName(Player.getX(),Player.getZ())+"\n"+"X : "+Math.floor(Player.getX())+" Y : "+Math.floor(Player.getY())+" Z : "+Math.floor(Player.getZ()));}catch(e){Matin.error(e);}}}));}if(MiniMap.window != null && MiniMap.time == 1) {ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run: function() {try {var mapData = MiniMap.createMapData();var back = new android.graphics.drawable.BitmapDrawable(mapData);back.setAlpha(200);MiniMap.data.setBackgroundDrawable(back);} catch(e) {clientMessage(e + ", " + e.lineNumber);}}}));MiniMap.time = 11;}if(MiniMap.time > 0) {MiniMap.time--;} if(차단tick==true&&Mmenu!=null) {Mmenu.dismiss();Mmenu = null;치치차단(); }if(bright==true){if(Player.getCarriedItem()==50){ //토치setTile(getPlayerX(), getPlayerY(), getPlayerZ(), 32);}if(Player.getCarriedItem()==325&&Player.getCarriedItemData()==10){ //용암양동이setTile(getPlayerX(), getPlayerY(), getPlayerZ(), 32); }if(Player.getCarriedItem()==89){//발광석setTile(getPlayerX(), getPlayerY(), getPlayerZ(), 32);}var x = Player.getX();var y = Player.getY();var z = Player.getZ();if(getTile(x-1,y,z)==32){setTile(x-1,y,z,0);}if(getTile(x+1,y,z)==32){setTile(x+1,y,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y,z-1)==32){setTile(x,y,z-1,0);}if(getTile(x,y,z+1)==32){setTile(x,y,z+1,0);}if(getTile(x-1,y,z+1)==32){setTile(x-1,y,z+1,0);}if(getTile(x-1,y,z-1)==32){setTile(x-1,y,z-1,0);}if(getTile(x+1,y,z+1)==32){setTile(x+1,y,z+1,0);}if(getTile(x+1,y,z-1)==32){setTile(x+1,y,z-1,0);}if(getTile(x,y-1,z)==32){setTile(x,y-1,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y+1,z)==32){setTile(x,y+1,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y+1,z)==32){setTile(x,y+1,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y+1,z)==32){setTile(x,y+1,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y+2,z)==32){setTile(x,y+2,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y+2,z)==32){setTile(x,y+2,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y+2,z)==32){setTile(x,y+2,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y+2,z)==32){setTile(x,y+2,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y+2,z)==32){setTile(x,y+2,z,0);}if(getTile(x+1,y+1,z)==32){setTile(x+1,y+1,z,0);}if(getTile(x-1,y+1,z)==32){setTile(x-1,y+1,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y+1,z+1)==32){setTile(x,y+1,z+1,0);}if(getTile(x,y+1,z-1)==32){setTile(x,y+1,z-1,0);}if(getTile(x+2,y+1,z)==32){setTile(x+2,y+1,z,0);}if(getTile(x-2,y+1,z)==32){setTile(x-2,y+1,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y+1,z+2)==32){setTile(x,y+1,z+2,0);}if(getTile(x,y+1,z-2)==32){setTile(x,y+1,z-2,0);}if(getTile(x+2,y,z)==32){setTile(x+2,y,z,0)}if(getTile(x-2,y,z)==32){setTile(x-2,y,z,0);}if(getTile(x,y,z+2)==32){setTile(x,y,z+2,0);}if(getTile(x,y,z-2)==32){setTile(x,y,z-2,0);}}var pls = ScriptManager.allplayers;for(var n = 0; function attackHook(a,v){if(a==getPlayerEnt()){if(hitEntityKill){Entity.setHealth(v,0);}if(armor==true) {preventDefault();ent=v;모자설정();armor=false;}if(stopEntity){Entity.setImmobile(v,true);stopEntity = false;}if(rideEntity){rideEntity = false;Entity.rideAnimal(a,v);}if(v&&mobt==0&&mobv==1) {preventDefault();clientMessage("§e몹매틀할 §a첫번째 §e대상이 정해졌습니다.");clientMessage("§e이젠 두번째 대상을 선택해 주세요");v1=v;mobt++;}else if(v&&mobt==1){preventDefault();clientMessage("§e몹배틀할 §a두번째 §e대상이 정해졌습니다.");clientMessage("§b몹배틀을 시작합니다!!");v2=v;Entity.setTarget(v1,v2);Entity.setTarget(v2,v1);mobv=0;mobt=0;}}if(HackFuck==true&&getCarriedItem()==0) {var ex=Entity.getX(v);var ey=Entity.getY(v);var ez=Entity.getZ(v);explode(ex,ey,ez,0.7);}var vil=1;var att=0;for(var q in player){if(player[q].ent==v)vil=player[q].team;if(player[q].ent==a)att=player[q].team;}if(att==vil){preventDefault();vil=1;att=0;}if(Player.isPlayer(a)) playerAddedHandler(a);if(Player.isPlayer(v)) playerAddedHandler(v);}
function playerAddedHandler(p) {var isLeft = false;if(leftPls[0] != null) {for(var n = 0; n < leftPls.length; n++) {if(leftPls[n] == p) {ScriptManager.callScriptMethod("entityAddedHook", [new java.lang.Long(p)]);ScriptManager.allplayers.add(new java.lang.Long(p));isLeft = true;ModPE.showTipMessage("\n\n들어온 플레이어를 인식하였습니다.\n닉네임 : " + Player.getName(p) + ", Client Id : " + p);leftPls.splice(n, 1);}}}if(!isLeft) {var checkDouble = false;var ents = ScriptManager.allentities;for(var n = 0; n < ents.size(); n++) {if(ents.get(n) == p) {checkDouble = true;break;}}if(!checkDouble) {ModPE.showTipMessage("\n\n새로운 플레이어를 인식하였습니다.\n닉네임 : " + Player.getName(p) + ", Client Id : " + p);ScriptManager.entityAddedCallback(new java.lang.Long(p));}}}
function entityAddedHook(ent){var entityId = Entity.getEntityTypeId(ent);if(noSpawnMob&&entityId==noSpawnMobId){Entity.remove(ent);}if(snfi&&Entity.getEntityTypeId(ent)==81){var a = Level.spawnMob(Entity.getX(ent), Entity.getY(ent), Entity.getZ(ent), 85);SS.push(a);Entity.rideAnimal(ent ,a);}if(antiTerror[0]&&entityId==65) Entity.remove(ent);if(antiTerror[2]&&entityId==52) Entity.remove(ent);}

function fixArray(arr, path, tf){var arr1 = [];var arr2 = [];var arr3 = [];for each(var ff in arr){if(ff.substring(0, 1)!=".")arr1.push(ff);}for each(var ff in arr1){var fff = new java.io.File(path+"/"+ff);var ffff = ff.split("\\.");var fffff = ffff[ffff.length-1];if(fff.isDirectory())arr2.push(ff);if((!tf&&(fffff=="mp3"||fffff=="wav"||fffff=="flac"||fffff=="aac"||fffff=="ogg"||fffff=="fsb"))||(tf&&fffff=="zip"))arr3.push(ff);}var arr4 = arr2.sort();var arr5 = arr3.sort();for each(var ff in arr5)arr4.push(ff)return arr4;}
function playMusic(path){ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run : function(){try{media.reset();media.setDataSource(path);media.prepare();media.start();Matin.toast("노래를 재생합니다.");}catch(e){clientMessage(e+","+e.lineNumber);}}}));}
function fileList(path, btn){ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run: function(){try{var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx);var dir = new java.io.File(path).list();var dir2 = fixArray(dir, path, false);dialog.setItems(dir2, new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({onClick : function(m, w){var dir3 = new java.io.File(path+"/"+dir2[w]);if(dir3.isDirectory()){fileList(dir3, btn);}else{playMusic(dir3);btn.setText("노래 정지");music = true;}}}));dialog.setTitle("듣고싶으신 노래파일을 선택해 주세요");dialog.setNegativeButton("취소", null);dialog.show();}catch(e){Matin.error(e);}}}));}
function listenSong(path, btn){ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run: function(){try{var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx);var dir = new java.io.File(path).list();var dir2 = fixArray(dir, path, false);dialog.setItems(dir2, new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({onClick : function(m, w){var dir3 = new java.io.File(path+"/"+dir2[w]);if(dir3.isDirectory()){fileList(dir3, btn);}else{playMusic(dir3);btn.setText("노래 정지");music = true;}}}));dialog.setTitle("듣고싶으신 노래파일을 선택해 주세요");dialog.setNegativeButton("취소", null);dialog.show();}catch(e){Matin.error(e);}}}));}
function weatherSet() {ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run: function() {try {var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx);var layout = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx);layout.setOrientation(1);var loc1 = new android.widget.TextView(ctx);var loc2 = new android.widget.SeekBar(ctx);var loc3 = new android.widget.TextView(ctx);var loc4 = new android.widget.SeekBar(ctx);var txt1 = Math.round(Level.getRainLevel() * 100);var txt2 = Math.round(Level.getLightningLevel() * 100);loc1.setText("비 강도 : " + (txt1 / 100));loc1.setTextColor(android.graphics.Color.BLACK);loc1.setTextSize(18);loc3.setText("번개 강도 : " + (txt2 / 100));  loc3.setTextColor(android.graphics.Color.BLACK);loc3.setTextSize(18);loc2.setMax(100);loc4.setMax(100);loc2.setProgress(txt1);loc4.setProgress(txt2);loc2.setOnSeekBarChangeListener(new android.widget.SeekBar.OnSeekBarChangeListener({onProgressChanged: function(seek) {loc1.setText("비 강도 : " + (seek.getProgress() / 100)); loc1.setTextColor(android.graphics.Color.BLACK); txt1 = seek.getProgress();}}));loc4.setOnSeekBarChangeListener(new android.widget.SeekBar.OnSeekBarChangeListener({onProgressChanged: function(seek) {loc3.setText("번개 강도 : " + (seek.getProgress() / 100));loc3.setTextColor(android.graphics.Color.BLACK);  txt2 = seek.getProgress();}}));loc1.setTextColor(android.graphics.Color.BLACK);  loc3.setTextColor(android.graphics.Color.BLACK);layout.addView(loc1);layout.addView(loc2);layout.addView(loc3);layout.addView(loc4);var pad = dip2px(ctx, 5);layout.setPadding(pad, pad, pad, pad);var scroll = new android.widget.ScrollView(ctx);scroll.addView(layout);dialog.setView(scroll);dialog.setTitle("날씨 상세 설정");dialog.setNegativeButton("설정 안함", null);dialog.setPositiveButton("설정 완료", new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({onClick: function(v) {Level.setRainLevel(txt1 / 100);Level.setLightningLevel(txt2 / 100);Matin.toast("날씨가 설정되었습니다.");}}));dialog.show();} catch(e) {Matin.toast(e);}}}));}

function getEnabledScriptsArray() {var prefs=com.mojang.minecraftpe.MainActivity.currentMainActivity.get().getSharedPreferences("mcpelauncherprefs",0);var scripts=prefs.getString("enabledScripts","");return scripts.split(";");}

function setItemName(){ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run: function(){try{var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx);var layout = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx);layout.setOrientation(1);var scroll = new android.widget.ScrollView(ctx);var name = new android.widget.EditText(ctx);noFullKeyboard(name);name.setInputType(android.text.InputType.TYPE_CLASS_TEXT);name.setHint(Item.getName(Player.getCarriedItem(),Player.getCarriedItemData()));Matin.noFullScreen(name);layout.addView(name);scroll.addView(layout);dialog.setView(scroll);dialog.setTitle("아이템 이름 변경");dialog.setMessage("들고있는 아이템의 이름을 변경합니다.");dialog.setNegativeButton("취소", null);dialog.setPositiveButton("확인", new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({onClick : function(v){Player.setItemCustomName(Player.getSelectedSlotId(), name.getText().toString());}}));dialog.show();}catch(e){Matin.error(e);}}}));}
function 인첸트해제() {var itemName = Player.getItemCustomName(Player.getSelectedSlotId());Entity.setCarriedItem(Player.getEntity(), getCarriedItem(), Player.getCarriedItemCount(), Player.getCarriedItemData());if(itemName!=null) Player.setItemCustomName(Player.getSelectedSlotId(), itemName);Matin.toast("인첸트가 해제되었습니다");}
function enchantDialog(){ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run: function(){try{var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx);var layout = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx);layout.setOrientation(1);var types = ["수중 호흡", "살충", "폭발 저항", "친수성", "효율", "가벼운 착지", "화염 검", "화염 보호", "화염 활", "행운", "무한", "밀치기", "약탈", "바다 행운", "미끼", "힘", "원거리 보호", "보호", "때리기", "호흡", "날카로움", "섬세한 손길", "강타", "가시", "내구성"];var typeId = new Array();var checks = new Array();for(var n in types){checks[n] = new android.widget.CheckBox(ctx);checks[n].setText(types[n]);checks[n].setId(n);checks[n].setOnCheckedChangeListener(new android.widget.CompoundButton.OnCheckedChangeListener({onCheckedChanged : function(check, onoff){if(onoff==true){typeId.push(check.getId());}else if(onoff==false){typeId.splice(typeId.indexOf(check.getId()), 1);}}}));layout.addView(checks[n]);}var scroll = android.widget.ScrollView(ctx);scroll.addView(layout);dialog.setView(scroll);dialog.setTitle("인첸트할 종류를 선택해 주세요");dialog.setNegativeButton("취소", null);dialog.setPositiveButton("확인", new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({onClick: function(v){enchantPower(typeId);}}));dialog.show();Matin.toast("참고 : 아이템마다 가능한 인첸트가 다릅니다.");}catch(e){clientMessage(e+", "+e.lineNumber);}}}));}
function enchantPower(typeId){ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run: function(){try{var type = [Enchantment.AQUA_AFFINITY, Enchantment.BANE_OF_ARTHROPODS, Enchantment.BLAST_PROTECTION, Enchantment.DEPTH_STRIDER, Enchantment.EFFICIENCY, Enchantment.FEATHER_FALLING, Enchantment.FIRE_ASPECT, Enchantment.FIRE_PROTECTION, Enchantment.FLAME, Enchantment.FORTUNE, Enchantment.INFINITY, Enchantment.KNOCKBACK, Enchantment.LOOTING, Enchantment.LUCK_OF_THE_SEA, Enchantment.LURE, Enchantment.POWER, Enchantment.PROJECTILE_PROTECTION, Enchantment.PROTECTION, Enchantment.PUNCH, Enchantment.RESPIRATION, Enchantment.SHARPNESS, Enchantment.SILK_TOUCH, Enchantment.SMITE, Enchantment.THORNS, Enchantment.UNBREAKING];var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx);var layout = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx);layout.setOrientation(1);layout.setGravity(android.view.Gravity.CENTER);var txt1 = new android.widget.TextView(ctx);txt1.setText("강도 설정");txt1.setTextSize(18);var txt2 = new android.widget.EditText(ctx);noFullKeyboard(txt2);txt2.setHint("강도를 설정해 주세요...");txt2.setInputType(android.text.InputType.TYPE_CLASS_NUMBER|android.text.InputType.TYPE_NUMBER_FLAG_SIGNED);layout.addView(txt1);layout.addView(txt2);var scroll = android.widget.ScrollView(ctx);scroll.addView(layout);dialog.setView(scroll);dialog.setTitle("인첸트할 강도를 적어 주세요");dialog.setNegativeButton("취소", null);dialog.setPositiveButton("확인", new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({onClick: function(v){for(var n in typeId){Player.enchant(Player.getSelectedSlotId(), type[typeId[n]], Number(txt2.getText()));}Matin.toast("인첸트 성공!");}}));dialog.show();}catch(e){clientMessage(e+", "+e.lineNumber);}}}));}

function fixXYZ() {we.min[0] = Math.min(we.x[0], we.x[1]);we.max[0] = Math.max(we.x[0], we.x[1]);we.min[1] = Math.min(we.y[0], we.y[1]);we.max[1] = Math.max(we.y[0], we.y[1]);we.min[2] = Math.min(we.z[0], we.z[1]);we.max[2] = Math.max(we.z[0], we.z[1]);}
var useBackUp = false;var backUpPeriod = 6000;var useThread = true;var time = 0;
const File = { save: function(path, msg){  try{   var file = new java.io.File(path);   var fos = new java.io.FileOutputStream(file);   var str = new java.lang.String(msg);   fos.write(str.getBytes());   fos.close();  }catch(e){   Matin.error(e);  } },copy: function(path1, path2) {try {var file1 = new java.io.File(path1);var file2 = new java.io.File(path2);var fis = new java.io.FileInputStream(file1).getChannel();var fos = new java.io.FileOutputStream(file2).getChannel();fis.transferTo(0, fis.size(), fos);fis.close();fos.close();} catch(e) {Matin.error(e);}},copyFolder: function(path1, path2) {try {var file1 = new java.io.File(path1);var file2 = new java.io.File(path2);if(file1.isDirectory()) {var file3 = new java.io.File(path2, file1.getName());file3.mkdirs();var child = file1.list();for(var n = 0; n < child.length; n++) {var file4 = new java.io.File(file1, child[n]);if(file4.isDirectory()) File.copyFolder(file4, file3);else File.copy(file4, new java.io.File(file3, child[n]));}} else {File.copy(path1, path2);}} catch(e) {Matin.error(e);}}};

Matin.toast("해당 지역의 "+n+"개의 블럭들을 삭제했습니다.");}if(Cmd == "테러제거"&&useWE==true||Cmd=="/antiTerror"&&useWE==true) {fixXYZ();var count = 0;for(var xx = posFixed1[0]; xx <= posFixed2[0]; xx++) {for(var yy = posFixed1[1]; yy <= posFixed2[1]; yy++) {for(var zz = posFixed1[2]; zz <= posFixed2[2]; zz++) {if([46, 407, 10, 11, 8, 9].indexOf(getTile(xx, yy, zz)) != -1) { //tnt. 용암. 물count++;setTile(xx, yy, zz, 0);}}}}
message(n+"개의 TNT, 물 그리고 용암을 제거했습니다");}if(Cmd == "월드에딧"&&useWE==true) { showDialog("월드에딧 명령어 목록","/아이템, /채우기(//set) [블록 아이디] [블록 데미지] : pos 1, pos 2 까지 되는 구역을 설정한 아이템으로 채웁니다\n/바꾸기(//replace) [블록 아이디1] [블록 아이디2] : pos 1, pos 2로 지정한 구역 중에 아이템 아이디가 [블록 아이디1]인 블록을 [블록 아이디2]로 바꿉니다\n/제거(//remove) : pos 1, pos 2로 지정한 구역을 없앱니다\n/테러제거(//antiTerror) : pos 1, pos 2로 지정한 구역에서 TNT, 용암, 물을 없앱니다.");}   }

var blockIds = [];var blockDamages = [];var lengths = [];
function WEcopy() { fixXYZ();  var n = 0, m = 0, o = 0;  var nn = 0;  blockIds = [];  blockDamages = [];  for(var xx = x1; xx < x2 + 1; xx++) {blockIds[n] = new Array(x2 - x1);blockDamages[n] = new Array(x2 - x1);for(var yy = y1; yy < y2 + 1; yy++) {  blockIds[n][m] = new Array(y2 - y1);  blockDamages[n][m] = new Array(y2 - y1);  for(var zz = z1; zz < z2 + 1; zz++) {blockIds[n][m][o] = new Array();blockDamages[n][m][o] = new Array();blockIds[n][m][o] = getTile(xx, yy, zz);blockDamages[n][m][o] = Level.getData(xx, yy, zz);o++;nn++;  }  lengths[2] = o;  o = 0;  m++;}lengths[1] = m;m = 0;n++;  }  lengths[0] = n;  Matin.toast(nn + "개의 블록들을 복사했습니다.");}
function WEpaste() { fixPosition();  var nn = 0;  for(var n = 0; n < lengths[0]; n++) {for(var m = 0; m < lengths[1]; m++) {  for(var o = 0; o < lengths[2]; o++) {setTile(x1 + n, y1 + m, z1 + o, blockIds[n][m][o], blockDamages[n][m][o]);nn++;  }}  }  Matin.toast(nn + "개의 블록들을 붙여넣었습니다.");}

ModPE.getText = function(url) {    try {        var url = new java.net.URL(url);        var con = url.openConnection();        if(con != null) {            con.setConnectTimeout(5000);            con.setUseCaches(false);            var isr = new java.io.InputStreamReader(con.getInputStream());            var br = new java.io.BufferedReader(isr);            var str = br.readLine();            var line = "";            while((line = br.readLine()) != null) {                str += "\n" + line;            }            isr.close();            br.close();            con.disconnect();        }        return str.toString();    } catch(e) {        clientMessage(e + ", " + e.lineNumber);    }};

function getTextFromWeb(url) {    try {        var url = new java.net.URL(url);        var con = url.openConnection();        if(con != null) {   con.setConnectTimeout(5000);            con.setUseCaches(false);            var isr = new java.io.InputStreamReader(con.getInputStream());            var br = new java.io.BufferedReader(isr);            var str = br.readLine();            var line = "";            while((line = br.readLine()) != null) {                str += "\n" + line;            }            isr.close();            br.close();            con.disconnect();        }        return str.toString();    } catch(e) {        clientMessage(e + ", " + e.lineNumber);    }};

ModPE.getText = function(url) {    try {        var url = new java.net.URL(url);        var con = url.openConnection();        if(con != null) {            con.setConnectTimeout(5000);            con.setUseCaches(false);            var isr = new java.io.InputStreamReader(con.getInputStream());            var br = new java.io.BufferedReader(isr);            var str = br.readLine();            var line = "";            while((line = br.readLine()) != null) {                str += "\n" + line;            }            isr.close();            br.close();            con.disconnect();        }        return str.toString();    } catch(e) {        clientMessage(e + ", " + e.lineNumber);    }};

function showMyIp(){try{var content = new java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream();android.net.http.AndroidHttpClient.newInstance("userAgent").execute(new org.apache.http.client.methods.HttpGet("http://ip-api.com/json")).getEntity().writeTo(content);content.close();return String(content.toString()).split("\"")[31];}catch(e){Matin.toast("오류 발생 : "+e+"\n인터넷 연결을 확인해주세요.");return;Matin.showError(e);}};

function introToast(msg, tf){ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run : function(){try{var toast = new android.widget.Toast.makeText(ctx, "<IntroToast> "+msg, android.widget.Toast.LENGTH_LONG);toast.getView().setBackgroundDrawable(new android.graphics.drawable.ColorDrawable(android.graphics.Color.argb(140, 30, 30, 30)));if(tf) toast.setGravity(android.view.Gravity.CENTER|android.view.Gravity.CENTER, 0, 0);if(tf=="top") toast.setGravity(android.view.Gravity.TOP|android.view.Gravity.TOP, 0, 0);toast.show();}catch(e){print(e);}}}));}
function carrotToast(msg){ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run : function(){try{var toast = new android.widget.Toast.makeText(ctx, "<CarrotToast> "+msg, android.widget.Toast.LENGTH_LONG);toast.getView().setBackgroundDrawable(new android.graphics.drawable.ColorDrawable(android.graphics.Color.argb(255, 255, 125, 50)));toast.setGravity(android.view.Gravity.CENTER|android.view.Gravity.CENTER, 0, 0);toast.show();}catch(e){print(e);}}}));}

function 치치차단(){ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run: function(){try{var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx);dialog.setTitle("스크립트 작동 차단");dialog.setMessage("무단 공유 또는 구버전의 이유로 인하여 제작자가 스크립트의 작동을 차단하였습니다.\n만약 구버전 때문에 차단된 경우에는 제작자 깃허브에서 신버전을 받으실수 있습니다.\n현재 버전 : "+version+"\n최신 버전 : "+newVersion);dialog.setNegativeButton("닫기", null);dialog.setPositiveButton("제작자 깃허브", new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({onClick: function(v){var uri = new android.net.Uri.parse("http://github.com/matin1202/chinacheaterversion");var link = new android.content.Intent(android.content.Intent.ACTION_VIEW, uri);ctx.startActivity(link);}}));dialog.show();dialog.setCancelable(false);}catch(e){Matin.error(e);}}}));차단tick=true;} 
function checkInterneter(){try{var cm = ctx.getSystemService(android.content.Context.CONNECTIVITY_SERVICE);var mobile = cm.getNetworkInfo(cm.TYPE_MOBILE);var wifi = cm.getNetworkInfo(cm.TYPE_WIFI);if(mobile.isConnected()||wifi.isConnected()){return true;}else{return false;}}catch(e){try{if(wifi.isConnected()){return true;}}catch(e){Matin.error(e);}}}
if(!checkInterneter()) introToast("need Wi-Fi","top"); Matin.makeButton();
function showNoticeDialog() {if(checkInterneter()) {ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run: function(){try{var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx);var layout = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx);layout.setOrientation(1);var web = new android.webkit.WebView(ctx);web.setWebChromeClient(new android.webkit.WebChromeClient());web.setWebViewClient(new android.webkit.WebViewClient());web.loadUrl("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/matin1202/Cheater/master/Noti");layout.addView(web);var scroll = new android.widget.ScrollView(ctx);scroll.addView(layout);dialog.setView(scroll);dialog.setTitle("China Cheater 공지 사항");dialog.setNegativeButton("닫기", null);dialog.show();}catch(e){Matin.error(e);}}}));}else {   Matin.toast("치치의 공지사항을 확인하기 위해서는 인터넷 연결이 필요합니다.\n인터넷 연결 확인후 다시 시도해 주세요!");}}
function checkNewVersion() {  if (checkInterneter()) {  if(version != newVersion) { showDialog("치치 최신버전 확인","현재 적용중인 치치 버전 : "+version+"\n치치 최신버전 : "+newVersion);  } else Matin.toast("이미 최신버전 입니다."); }}
function reg() {   if(checkInterneter()) showRegDialog();  else Matin.toast("인터넷 연결이 필요합니다!");}
ModPE.getMyIp = function(){try{var content = new java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream();android.net.http.AndroidHttpClient.newInstance("userAgent").execute(new org.apache.http.client.methods.HttpGet("http://ip-api.com/json")).getEntity().writeTo(content);content.close();return String(content.toString()).split("\"")[31];}catch(e){Matin.toast("오류 발생 : "+e+"\n인터넷 연결을 확인해주세요.");return;Matin.error(e);}};

function appInstalled(pack) {var installed = false;var pm = com.mojang.minecraftpe.MainActivity.currentMainActivity.get().getPackageManager();try {pm.getPackageInfo(pack, android.content.pm.PackageManager.GET_ACTIVITIES);installed = true;}catch(e) {installed = false;}return installed;}
function installApk(path) {var intent = new android.content.Intent(android.content.Intent.ACTION_VIEW);intent.setDataAndType(new android.net.Uri.parse("file://"+path), "application/vnd.android.package-archive");ctx.startActivity(intent);}
function CCaddon() {if(appInstalled("gravity.minecraft.app.rpg.script")) {   Matin.toast("당신은 C.C. Addon을 사용할 준비가 다 되었습니다!");  Matin.toast("RPG 스크립트 앱을 열어서 실행시켜 주세요!");}else {Matin.toast("당신은 C.C. Addon이 깔려있지 않습니다!");addonDownloadDialog();}}
function makeRPGtitle(text){var Title = new android.widget.TextView(ctx);Title.setText(text);Title.setTextColor(White);Title.setTextSize(15);Title.setGravity(Center);return Title;}
function showMemo(){ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run: function(){try{RPGtitle = new android.widget.PopupWindow();var layout = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx);var layout2 = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx);var scroll = new android.widget.ScrollView(ctx);var title = makeRPGtitle("Memo\n");title.setLayoutParams(new android.widget.LinearLayout.LayoutParams(android.widget.LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, android.widget.LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT));var menus = ["메모 쓰기","메모 읽기","최소화","닫기"], btns = [];for(var i in menus){btns[i] = new android.widget.Button(ctx);btns[i].setText(menus[i]);btns[i].setTextColor(White);btns[i].setId(i);btns[i].setLayoutParams(new android.widget.LinearLayout.LayoutParams(android.widget.LinearLayout.LayoutParams.MATCH_PARENT, android.widget.LinearLayout.LayoutParams.WRAP_CONTENT))btns[i].setBackgroundDrawable(new android.graphics.drawable.ColorDrawable(BBack));layout2.addView(btns[i]);
btns[i].setOnClickListener(new android.view.View.OnClickListener(){onClick : function(v){switch(v.getId()){case 0:writeMemo();break;case 1 :if(nicknameTitle=="일반"){try{showDialog("일반 회원 메모장",Matin.read("memo"));}catch(e){Matin.error(e);}}else readVIPmemo();break;case 2 :Matin.toast("타이틀을 눌러주세요.");break;case 3 :RPGtitle.dismiss();break;}}});}
title.setOnClickListener(new android.view.View.OnClickListener(){onClick : function(v){if(layout2.getVisibility()==android.view.View.INVISIBLE) layout2.setVisibility(android.view.View.VISIBLE), RPGtitle.update(dip2px(ctx, 100), dip2px(ctx, 200));else layout2.setVisibility(android.view.View.INVISIBLE), RPGtitle.update(dip2px(ctx, 100), dip2px(ctx, 20));}});
layout2.setVisibility(android.view.View.INVISIBLE);layout.setOrientation(layout.VERTICAL);layout2.setOrientation(layout2.VERTICAL);layout2.setGravity(Right | Top);layout2.setPadding(0, 9, 0, 9);layout.addView(title);scroll.addView(layout2);layout.addView(scroll);RPGtitle.setContentView(layout);RPGtitle.setBackgroundDrawable(new android.graphics.drawable.ColorDrawable(BBack));Matin.sdr(title, RPGtitle);RPGtitle.setWidth(dip2px(ctx, 100));RPGtitle.setHeight(dip2px(ctx, 20));RPGtitle.showAtLocation(ctx.getWindow().getDecorView(),Left|Center, 9, 9);}catch(e){RPG.error(e);}}}));}
function deleteMemo(){  RPGtitle.dismiss();}
function writeMemo() { useMemoPassword = false;ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run : function(){ try{  var isPassWord = false;var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx); var layoutgmc = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx); layoutgmc.setOrientation(1); layoutgmc.setGravity(android.view.Gravity.CENTER);   var loc1 = new android.widget.TextView(ctx);  var loc2 = new android.widget.EditText(ctx); noFullKeyboard(loc2);var loc3 = new android.widget.TextView(ctx);  var loc4 = new android.widget.EditText(ctx); noFullKeyboard(loc4);var loc5 = new android.widget.TextView(ctx);  var loc6 = new android.widget.EditText(ctx); noFullKeyboard(loc6);var loc7 = new android.widget.Switch(ctx);
loc1.setText("["+nicknameTitle+"] 메모장 제목 : "); loc1.setTextSize(20);  loc2.setHint("메모장의 제목을 입력해 주세요..."); loc3.setText("메모장 내용 : "); loc3.setTextSize(20);  loc4.setHint("메모장의 내용을 입력해 주세요..."); loc5.setText("["+nicknameTitle+"] 메모장 비밀번호 : "); loc5.setTextSize(20);  loc6.setHint("만약 비밀번호를 없이 하고싶다면 비밀번호 작성칸을 비워주세요."); loc7.setText("암호 잠금 사용");loc7.setChecked(false);loc7.setTextOn("");loc7.setTextOff("");loc7.setOnCheckedChangeListener(new android.widget.CompoundButton.OnCheckedChangeListener({onCheckedChanged: function(swit, isChecked) {if(isChecked) {useMemoPassword = true;} else {useMemoPassword = false;}}}));   
if(nicknameTitle=="VIP"||nicknameTitle=="VVIP") layoutgmc.addView(loc1);  if(nicknameTitle=="VIP"||nicknameTitle=="VVIP") layoutgmc.addView(loc2);
layoutgmc.addView(loc3);layoutgmc.addView(loc4);
if(nicknameTitle=="VIP"||nicknameTitle=="VVIP") layoutgmc.addView(loc7); 
var scroll = new android.widget.ScrollView(ctx); scroll.addView(layoutgmc); dialog.setView(scroll);  dialog.setTitle("메모장"); dialog.setNegativeButton("취소", null);  dialog.setPositiveButton("저장", new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({onClick: function(v){if(nicknameTitle=="일반") {Matin.toast("VIP 회원은 메모장의 제목과 비밀번호를 설정할수 있습니다.");Matin.toast("메모장이 저장되었습니다!");Matin.save("memo",loc4.getText());}if(nicknameTitle=="VIP"||nicknameTitle=="VVIP") {Matin.toast("["+nicknameTitle+"] 메모장이 저장되었습니다!");Matin.save("memoTitle",loc2.getText());Matin.save("memoText",loc4.getText());if(useMemoPassword==true) setMemoPassword();if(useMemoPassword==false) Matin.save("memoPassword","false");}}}));  dialog.show();  }catch(e){  Matin.error(e);}}}));  }
function setMemoPassword() {Matin.toast("비밀번호를 설정해 주세요.");ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run : function(){ try{  var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx); var layoutgmc = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx); layoutgmc.setOrientation(1); layoutgmc.setGravity(android.view.Gravity.CENTER);   var loc1 = new android.widget.TextView(ctx);  var loc2 = new android.widget.EditText(ctx); noFullKeyboard(loc2);loc1.setText("설정할 비밀번호 : "); loc1.setTextSize(20);  loc2.setHint("비밀번호를 false로 적으시면 암호 잠금이 비활성화 됩니다...");
layoutgmc.addView(loc1);  layoutgmc.addView(loc2);
var scroll = new android.widget.ScrollView(ctx); scroll.addView(layoutgmc); dialog.setView(scroll);  dialog.setTitle("메모 비밀번호 설정"); dialog.setNegativeButton("취소", null);  dialog.setPositiveButton("설정 완료", new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({onClick: function(v){Matin.save("memoPassword",loc2.getText());Matin.toast("비밀번호가 설정되었습니다.");}}));  dialog.show();  }catch(e){  Matin.error(e);}}}));  }
function readVIPmemo() {if(Matin.read("memoPassword")=="false"||Matin.read("memoPassword")=="") {showDialog(Matin.read("memoTitle"),Matin.read("memoText"));}else checkMemoPassword();}
function checkMemoPassword(){ ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({run : function(){ try{  var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx); var layoutgmc = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx); layoutgmc.setOrientation(1); layoutgmc.setGravity(android.view.Gravity.CENTER);   var loc1 = new android.widget.TextView(ctx);  var loc2 = new android.widget.EditText(ctx); noFullKeyboard(loc2);loc1.setText("메모장에 비밀번호가 설정되어 있습니다!"); loc1.setTextColor(Red);loc1.setTextSize(25);  loc2.setHint("메모장을 열기 위한 비밀번호를 입력해 주세요...");
layoutgmc.addView(loc1);  layoutgmc.addView(loc2);
var scroll = new android.widget.ScrollView(ctx); scroll.addView(layoutgmc); dialog.setView(scroll);  dialog.setTitle("메모장이 잠겨 있습니다!"); dialog.setNegativeButton("취소", null);  dialog.setPositiveButton("비밀번호 확인", new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({onClick: function(v){if(loc2.getText().toString()==Matin.read("memoPassword")) {showDialog(Matin.read("memoTitle"),Matin.read("memoText"));}else if(loc2.getText()!==Matin.read("memoPassword").toString()) { Matin.toast("메모장에 설정되있는 비밀번호와 입력된 비밀번호가 다릅니다!"); }}}));  dialog.show();  }catch(e){  Matin.error(e);}}}));  }

function selectBlockLauncher(){ ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({  run: function(){   try{    var launcherType = "free";    var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx);    var layout = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx);    layout.setOrientation(1);    var radios = new android.widget.RadioGroup(ctx);    var menus = ["Block Launcher", "Block Launcher pro"];    var radio = [];    for(var n in menus){      radio[n] = new android.widget.RadioButton(ctx);     radio[n].setText(menus[n]);     radio[n].setId(n);     radios.addView(radio[n]);    }    radios.setOnCheckedChangeListener(new android.widget.RadioGroup.OnCheckedChangeListener({     onCheckedChanged: function(g, id){      if(id==0){       launcherType = "free";      }      else{       launcherType = "pro";      }     }    }));    var text = new android.widget.TextView(ctx);    text.setText("루팅(탈옥)을 하지 않았을시 Block Launcher에서 Block Launcher pro의 스크립트를 Block Launcher pro에서 Block Launcher의 스크립트를 확인하지 못합니다. 이점 유의하시길 바랍니다.");    text.setTextSize(20);    layout.addView(text);    layout.addView(radios);    var scroll = new android.widget.ScrollView(ctx);    scroll.addView(layout);    dialog.setView(scroll);    dialog.setTitle("런처 타입 선택");    dialog.setNegativeButton("취소", null);    dialog.setPositiveButton("선택", new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({     onClick: function(v){      showScripts(launcherType);     }    }));    dialog.show();   }catch(e){    Matin.error(e);   }  } }));}
function showScripts(lt){ ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({  run: function(){   try{    var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx);    if(lt=="free") var path = "/data/data/net.zhuoweizhang.mcpelauncher/app_modscripts";    if(lt=="pro") var path = "/data/data/net.zhuoweizhang.mcpelauncher.pro/app_modscripts";    var file = new java.io.File(path).list().sort();    dialog.setItems(file, new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({     onClick: function(m, id){      openEditor(readScriptFile(file[id], lt), file[id], lt);      Matin.toast("에디터를 엽니다.");     }    }));    dialog.setTitle("스크립트 목록및 편집 대상 선택");    dialog.setNegativeButton("취소", null);    dialog.show();   }catch(e){    Matin.error("루팅(탈옥) 여부를 확인해주세요."+e);   }  } }));}
function openEditor(txt, name, lt){ ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({  run: function(){   try{    var dialog = new android.app.AlertDialog.Builder(ctx);    var layout = new android.widget.LinearLayout(ctx);    layout.setOrientation(1);    var editor = new android.widget.EditText(ctx);    editor.setText(txt);    editor.setTextSize(18);    layout.addView(editor);    Matin.noFullScreen(editor);    var scroll = new android.widget.ScrollView(ctx);    scroll.addView(layout);    dialog.setView(scroll);    dialog.setTitle("스크립트 에디터");    dialog.setNegativeButton("취소", null);    dialog.setPositiveButton("저장 및불러오기", new android.content.DialogInterface.OnClickListener({     onClick: function(v){      saveScript(editor.getText().toString(), name, lt);      Matin.toast(name+"을/를 수정합니다.\n재접속시 스크립트가 수정판으로 적용됩니다.");     }    }));    dialog.show();   }catch(e){    Matin.error(e);   }  } }));}
function saveScript(txt, name, lt){ try{  if(lt=="free") var path = "/data/data/net.zhuoweizhang.mcpelauncher/app_modscripts";  if(lt=="pro") var path = "/data/data/net.zhuoweizhang.mcpelauncher.pro/app_modscripts";  var file = new java.io.File(path+"/"+name);  var fileOutput = new java.io.FileOutputStream(file);  var msg = new java.lang.String(txt);  fileOutput.write(msg.getBytes());  fileOutput.close(); }catch(e){  Matin.error(e); }}
function readScriptFile(name, lt){ try{  if(lt=="free") var path = "/data/data/net.zhuoweizhang.mcpelauncher/app_modscripts";  if(lt=="pro") var path = "/data/data/net.zhuoweizhang.mcpelauncher.pro/app_modscripts";  var script = new java.io.File(path+"/"+name);  if(!script.exists()) return "";  var fileInput = new java.io.FileInputStream(script);  var input = new java.io.InputStreamReader(fileInput);  var buffer = new java.io.BufferedReader(input);  var msg = buffer.readLine();  var str = "";  while((str = buffer.readLine())!=null){   msg += "\n"+str;  }  fileInput.close();  input.close();  buffer.close();  return msg; }catch(e){  Matin.error(e); }}
function levelDat(){ try{  var file = new java.io.File(sdcard+"/games/com.mojang/minecraftWorlds/"+Level.getWorldDir()+"/level.dat");  if(!(file.exists())) return "";  var fis = new java.io.FileInputStream(file);  var isr = new java.io.InputStreamReader(fis);  var br = new java.io.BufferedReader(isr);  var str = br.readLine();  var line = "";  while((line = br.readLine()) != null){   str += "\n" + line;  }  fis.close();  isr.close();  br.close();  return str.toString();}catch(e){Matin.error(e);}}

function speed(onoff){ ctx.runOnUiThread(new java.lang.Runnable({  run: ()=>{   try{    if(!onoff) speedBtn[0].dismiss(); speedBtn[0] = null;    speedBtn[0] = new android.widget.PopupWindow();    speedBtn[1] = new android.widget.TextView(ctx);    speedBtn[1].setText("");    speedBtn[0].setContentView(speedBtn[1]);    speedBtn[0].setWidth(-2);    speedBtn[0].setHeight(-2);    speedBtn[0].showAtLocation(ctx.getWindow().getDecorView(), android.view.Gravity.CENTER|android.view.Gravity.LEFT, 0, 0);   }catch(e){    Matin.error(e);   }  } }));}
